[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue description  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing with Jazzer and libFuzzer, the target application did not [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplete processing within the allotted timeout. Instead of throwing an error or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception, the fuzzer simply reached its time limit and reported “ERROR: libFuzzer:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimeout.” The full thread dump shows the only active work occurring on the “main” [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthread, which is stuck in `org.apache.tika.parser.csv.CellFormatter.format` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequently in `TextAndCSVParser.parse`.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observed vulnerability type  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This behavior corresponds to a denial-of-service [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDoS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m style issue where [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munexpected or malicious input causes the parser to hang or enter a very long [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution path, exhausting the fuzzer’s time budget.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The main thread’s stack trace bottoms out in `CellFormatter.format` at line [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggesting that some [0m[1;35minput[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m cause the formatter to loop or stall indefinitely.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The CSV parsing entry point invoked by the fuzzer harness is [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVParser.parse`, which calls into the cell formatting logic.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other threads are blocked waiting on locks held by the main thread; they are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmostly garbage-collection and JVM housekeeping threads running normally.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • There is no exception or crash, indicating that the code is not throwing but [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather consuming time without termination.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/TextAndCSVParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:192[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m200[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:            try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:                for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCSVRecord row : commonsParser[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mxhtmlContentHandler.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTR[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:                    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell : row[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotalRows == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The hang originates in [0m[1;35mCellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where, for a matched [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“&fraction_format” directive, it computes all numerator/denominator pairs up to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength−[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m via nested for-loops [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Since [0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe as high as [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m overflows to a huge int [0m[1;39m([0m[39m≈Integer.MAX_VALUE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaking the loops effectively unbounded and causing the DoS.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy Overview  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We need to bound or short-circuit that brute-force search so that even [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madversarial inputs cannot trigger astronomic iterations, without impacting normal [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse. Specifically:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Short-circuit when the fractional part is zero [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno need for the search at [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Impose a small maximum on denomFormat length [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. ≤[0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to cap the search [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspace.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Introduce an early exit from the nested loops when an exact match is found [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[33mdiff[0m[39m==[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In org.apache.tika.parser.csv.CellFormatter:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Define a new constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnear line [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int MAX_DENOM_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In [0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, immediately after computing:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        double wholePart = …;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        double decPart   = …;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        int denomLength  = [0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      insert:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m If there's no fractional component, simply format the whole part.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecPart == [0m[1;36m0.[0m[39m0d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            String safeSign        = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msign == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[32m""[0m[39m : sign;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            String [0m[33msafeWholeFormat[0m[39m= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwholeFormat == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m? [0m[32m"#"[0m[39m : wholeFormat;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            NumberFormat wf        = new [0m[1;35mDecimalFormat[0m[1;39m([0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                     safeWholeFormat,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                     new [0m[1;35mDecimalFormatSymbols[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLocale.US[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return safeSign + [0m[1;35mwf.format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mwholePart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Reject overly large denominators to bound runtime.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenomLength > MAX_DENOM_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Too expensive to compute; leave cell unmodified.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return cell;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Refactor the brute-force loops [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to include:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - A labeled outer loop so we can break both loops when we find an exact [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatch.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Use the already-bounded denomLength to compute maxDenom = [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength−[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafely.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      outer:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = maxDenom; i > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i2 = maxDenom; i2 >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i2--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              double diff = [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi2 [0m[35m/[0m[39m i - decPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdiff < minVal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  currDenom = i;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  currNum   = i2;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  minVal    = diff;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdiff == [0m[1;36m0.[0m[39m0d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Perfect match – stop searching.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      break outer;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Impact  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The MAX_DENOM_LENGTH guard ensures worst-case loop count is [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterations, which is acceptable and bounds resource usage.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The [0m[33mdecPart[0m[39m==[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m short-circuit avoids unnecessary work when formatting whole [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumbers.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Breaking on an exact match optimizes common cases [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m0.5[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other formatting [0m[1;39m([0m[39mregex matching, number-format setup, CSV parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains unchanged.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to harness, tests, or external dependencies. Existing logic for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msmall fractions is preserved, and only pathological inputs are safely rejected.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side-Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inputs requesting extremely fine denominators [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will no longer be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatted as fractions; they will be returned verbatim. To document, update Javadoc[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto note the maximum supported denominator precision.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Routine performance overhead is negligible [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma quick length check and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzero-check[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unit tests covering fraction formatting should be updated [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor extended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minclude boundary cases: zero fractional part, maximum allowed denominator length, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand above-threshold behavior.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Next Steps  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Implement the patch in CellFormatter.java as described.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add new unit tests for:  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • fraction_format directives with no decimal part  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • denomFormat lengths at, below, and above MAX_DENOM_LENGTH  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run full CSV parser test suite to validate no regressions.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document the change in the release notes for users relying on high-precision [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfraction formatting.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
